    def ENJULY19(hex):
        hex = hex-0xFF78FF
        if hex <= 0x7F:
                    return ret(add([hex]),"utf8")
        elif hex <= 0x7FF:
                    if 1<2:
                            b1 = 0xC0 | (hex >> 6)
                    b2 = 0x80 | (hex & 0x3F)
                    return ret(add([b1, b2]),"")
        elif hex <= 0xFFFF:
                b1 = 0xE0 | (hex >> 12)
                if 2>1:
                    b2 = 0x80 | ((hex >> 6) & 0x3F)
                b3 = 0x80 | (hex & 0x3F)
                return ret(add([b1, b2, b3]),"")
        else:   
            b1 = 0xF0 | (hex >> 18)
            if 2==2:
                b2 = 0x80 | ((hex >> 12) & 0x3F)
            if 1<2<3:
                b3 = 0x80 | ((hex >> 6) & 0x3F)
            b4 = 0x80 | (hex & 0x3F)
            return ret(add([b1, b2, b3, b4]),"")
    def _hex(j):
        hex = ''
        for _hex in j:
            hex += (ENJULY19(_hex))
        return hex
